```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[MilestoneReferencesButton Component] --> B[Initialize State]
    B --> C{showModal = false}
    C --> D[useMemo: Create Columns]
    D --> E[Name Column]
    D --> F[Value Column]
    F --> G{Check qualifier type}
    G -->|ship to/from| H[Render LocationAddressComplex]
    G -->|other| I[Render Text with value]
    D --> J[Build referenceData array]
    J --> K{statusUpdate.references exists?}
    K -->|yes| L[Map references with capitalize]
    K -->|no| M[Empty array]
    L --> N{comments exists?}
    M --> N
    N -->|yes| O[Push comments to referenceData]
    N -->|no| P[Render Component]
    O --> P
    P --> Q[Outer div with stopPropagation]
    Q --> R[Icon Button]
    R -->|onClick| S[setShowModal true]
    S --> T[Modal Opens]
    T --> U[Modal Header: Milestone References]
    T --> V[Modal Body: BaseTable]
    V --> W[Display referenceData in table]
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[Props: statusUpdate, comments] --> B[MilestoneReferencesButton]
    B --> C[State: showModal]
    B --> D[Hook: useTranslation]
    B --> E[Computed: milestoneReferencesColumns]
    B --> F[Computed: referenceData]
    E --> G[BaseTable columns prop]
    F --> G[BaseTable data prop]
    G --> H[Modal Body]
    C --> I[Modal show prop]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class MilestoneReferencesButton {
        +statusUpdate: object
        +comments: string
        -showModal: boolean
        -t: function
        -milestoneReferencesColumns: array
        -referenceData: array
        +render()
    }
    class Modal {
        +show: boolean
        +onHide: function
        +backdrop: string
    }
    class ModalHeader {
        +closeButton: boolean
        +title: string
        +css: object
    }
    class ModalBody {
    }
    class BaseTable {
        +data: array
        +columns: array
        +theme: string
        +pageSize: number
        +disableSortBy: boolean
        +defaultSortColumn: string
        +defaultReverseSort: boolean
    }
    class Icon {
        +src: object
        +size: string
        +css: object
    }
    class LocationAddressComplex {
        +name: object
        +address1: string
        +address2: string
        +city: string
        +state: string
        +postalCode: string
        +country: string
    }
    class Text {
        +children: string
    }
    
    MilestoneReferencesButton --> Modal
    Modal --> ModalHeader
    Modal --> ModalBody
    ModalBody --> BaseTable
    MilestoneReferencesButton --> Icon
    BaseTable --> LocationAddressComplex
    BaseTable --> Text
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant Component as MilestoneReferencesButton
    participant State
    participant Modal
    participant BaseTable
    
    User->>Component: Mount with props
    Component->>State: Initialize showModal = false
    Component->>Component: useMemo milestoneReferencesColumns
    Component->>Component: Build referenceData from props
    Component->>User: Render Icon Button
    User->>Component: Click Icon
    Component->>State: setShowModal(true)
    State->>Modal: show = true
    Modal->>User: Display Modal
    Modal->>BaseTable: Pass data & columns
    BaseTable->>User: Display Table with References
    User->>Modal: Click close
    Modal->>Component: onHide callback
    Component->>State: setShowModal(false)
    State->>Modal: show = false
    Modal->>User: Hide Modal
```
